Each pair of functions are called before (enter function) and after (leave) a type M\+PI call. Which pair depends on the type of the call, and the functions called are E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+P\+Y\+\_\+$<$call$>$\+\_\+enter and leave. \index{M\+P\+I\+\_\+interface\+F.\+c@{M\+P\+I\+\_\+interface\+F.\+c}!E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+P\+I\+\_\+\+Allgather\+\_\+\+F\+\_\+leave@{E\+A\+R\+\_\+\+M\+P\+I\+\_\+\+Allgather\+\_\+\+F\+\_\+leave}}
